Anonymous Wikipedia edits from the German parliament and government

This is a list of anonymous edits of en.wikipedia.org made from the IP addresses of the German parliament and government from 2003-2014 (other sources). A total of 3015 edits were found. The data comes from dumps.wikimedia.org.

You can download the raw data used for this page as CSV or see the IP ranges used to find the edits.

Questions? Email or tweet me.

You can also donate through or to help me pay my Google BigQuery bill.

Follow @bundesedit

Please note that the IP ranges used are best effort attempts and may be inaccurate or incomplete. Any controversial edits you find should be independently verified.

Please contact the account owner if you have corrections to the ranges used.
